  ngAfterViewInit(): void {
    this.scrtable.sortObservable.subscribe((event) => {this.sortData(null,1)});
    this.pstable.sortObservable.subscribe((event) => {this.sortData(null,0)});

  refreshusers(site) {

    });

  _sortData(dd1: any, dd2: any, params: string[], dirs: string[]): number {
    const d1=dd1 as any;
    const d2=dd2 as any;
    
    if(params[0] =='appointmentDate' || params[0] =='callDate' || params[0] =='dateScheduledRecency'  ) {
      if (new Date(d1[params[0]]).getTime() > new Date(d2[params[0]]).getTime()) {
        return dirs[0] === 'asc' ? 1 : -1;
    } else if (new Date(d1[params[0]]).getTime() < new Date(d2[params[0]]).getTime()) {
      return dirs[0] === 'asc' ? -1 : 1;
  }  else {
        if (params.length > 1) {
            params = params.slice(1, params.length);
            dirs = dirs.slice(1, dirs.length);
            return this._sortData(d1, d2, params, dirs);
        } else {
            return 0;
        }
      }
    } else {
      
      if (d1[params[0]]?.toLowerCase() > d2[params[0]]?.toLowerCase()) {
        return dirs[0] === 'asc' ? 1 : -1;
    } else if (d1[params[0]]?.toLowerCase() < d2[params[0]]?.toLowerCase()) {
        return dirs[0] === 'asc' ? -1 : 1;
    } else {
        if (params.length > 1) {
            params = params.slice(1, params.length);
            dirs = dirs.slice(1, dirs.length);
            return this._sortData(d1, d2, params, dirs);
        } else {
            return 0;
        }
      }
    }
  }
  getReasons(event) {
    if(event.value == 0) {
      this.patientService.getReasonCategories().subscribe(res => {
        this.reasons = res.sort((a,b)=> this.compare(a?.name?.toLowerCase() , b?.name?.toLowerCase(),true));
      })
    } else {
      this.patientService.getActiveReasonCategoriesByApptType(event.value).subscribe(res => {
        this.reasons = res.sort((a,b)=> this.compare(a?.name?.toLowerCase() , b?.name?.toLowerCase(),true));
      })
    }
  }
  process(input){
  
    let value = input?.target?.value;
    let numbers = value.replace(/[^0-9]/g, );
    input.value = numbers;
  }

  toggleAllSelectionallsitestriagebyindication(status) {
  this.alltriagebyindication = status.selected
  if(this.alltriagebyindication) {
    status.select()
  } else {
      status.deselect()
  
    }
  if (this.alltriagebyindication) {
    this.reportForm.controls.siteidstriagebyindication
    .patchValue([...this.sites.map(item => item.id),0]);
    this.reportForm.controls.siteidstriagebyindication.updateValueAndValidity();

  } else {
    this.reportForm.controls.siteidstriagebyindication.patchValue([this.sites[0].id]);
    this.reportForm.controls.siteidstriagebyindication.updateValueAndValidity();
  }
}

  toggleTableRows() {
    this.isTableExpanded = !this.isTableExpanded;
    this.isTableExpanded2 = !this.isTableExpanded2;

    this.dataSource.data.forEach((row: any) => {
      row.isExpanded = this.isTableExpanded;
    })
    this.dataSource2.data.forEach((row: any) => {
      row.isExpanded = this.isTableExpanded2;
    })
  }
  
  searcher3 = (search: string, pageNumber: number, pageSize: number):Observable<any[]> => {
    if(search ==''){
      this.selectedIndications = []
    }
    const data = {
      search,
      pageNumber: pageNumber-1,
      pageSize,
    }
    if(pageNumber - 1 != 0) {
      this.sccipService.getindIcationsPaginated(data).subscribe(res => {
        res.content.forEach(element => {
            this.indications.push(element);
        });
      })
    } else {
      this.sccipService.getindIcationsPaginated(data).subscribe(res => {
        this.indications = res.content;
      })
    }
    return of(this.indications)
  }
  searcher2 = (search: any, pageNumber: number, pageSize: number):Observable<any[]> => { 
  
  this.studiesloading=true
  if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value =='STUDY_PARTICIPANTS_REPORT'){
    const data = {
      search: search,
      siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
      trialType: '',
      dateFrom:  '',
      dateTo: '',
      pageNumber: pageNumber-1,
      pageSize,
      studyId:''
    }
    if(pageNumber - 1 != 0) {
      this.advertisingService.getStudiesLastActivityPaginated(data).subscribe(res => {
        res.forEach(element => {
            this.studyLastActivity.push(element);
        });
      })
    } else {
      this.advertisingService.getStudiesLastActivityPaginated(data).subscribe(res => {
        this.studyLastActivity = res;
      })
    }
    this.studiesloading = false;
    return of(this.studyLastActivity)
  } else if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value =='VISIT_PROJECTIONS_REPORT') {
    let temp = []
    if(search == '') {
        this.studyLastActivity = this.studyLastActivityCopy;
    } else {
        this.studyLastActivityCopy.map(elem => {
            if(elem?.name?.toLowerCase().indexOf(search.toLowerCase()) > -1  ) {
                temp.push(elem);
            }
        });
        this.studyLastActivity = temp;
    }
    this.studiesloading = false;
    return of(this.studyLastActivity)
  }  else {
    const data = {
      siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
      trialType: '',
      dateFrom: this.alldates ?  formatDate(new Date().setFullYear(2000), 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') : this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us'),
      dateTo:this.alldates ?  formatDate(new Date(), 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') : this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us'),
      search: search,
      pageNumber: pageNumber-1,
      pageSize,
      studyId:''

    }
    if(pageNumber - 1 != 0) {
      this.advertisingService.getStudiesLastActivityPaginated(data).subscribe(res => {
        res.forEach(element => {
            this.studyLastActivity.push(element);
        });
      })
    } else {
      this.advertisingService.getStudiesLastActivityPaginated(data).subscribe(res => {
        this.studyLastActivity = res;
      })
    }
    this.studiesloading = false;
    return of(this.studyLastActivity)
  } 
   
  } 
  searcherclosed = (search: any, pageNumber: number, pageSize: number):Observable<any[]> => { 
  
  
  this.studiesloading=true
  let temp = []
  if(search == '') {
      this.studyLastActivity = this.studyLastActivityCopy;
  } else {
      this.studyLastActivityCopy.map(elem => {
          if(elem?.name?.toLowerCase().indexOf(search.toLowerCase()) > -1  ) {
              temp.push(elem);
          }
      });
      this.studyLastActivity = temp;
  }
  this.studiesloading = false;

  return of(this.studyLastActivity)
   
  }
  searcher2222 = (search: string, pageNumber: number, pageSize: number):Observable<any[]> => { 

    if(pageNumber - 1 != 0) {
      this.appointmentService.getDenovoStudies({pageSize:200,pageNumber:0,siteId:this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,statuses:['MOVING_FORWARD','ACTIVE'],search:''}).subscribe(res => {
        res.forEach(element => {
            this.studyLastActivity.push(element);
        });
      })
    } else {
      this.appointmentService.getDenovoStudies({pageSize:200,pageNumber:0,siteId:this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,statuses:['MOVING_FORWARD','ACTIVE'],search:''}).subscribe(res => {
        this.studyLastActivity = res;
      })
    }
    this.studiesloading = false;
    return of(this.studyLastActivity)
  }

      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.updateValueAndValidity();
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.setValue(JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('scUserSettings'))?.reportsDateTo== undefined ? '' :new Date(JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('scUserSettings'))?.reportsDateTo))
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.setValidators(null)
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.updateValueAndValidity();
      this.reportForm.controls.study.setValidators(null)
      this.reportForm.controls.study.updateValueAndValidity();   
      this.reportForm.controls.siteidsstudystartup.setValidators(null)
      this.reportForm.controls.siteidsstudystartup.updateValueAndValidity();
      this.reportForm.controls.siteidstriagebyindication.setValidators(Validators.required)
      this.reportForm.controls.siteidstriagebyindication.setValue([0])
      this.reportForm.controls.siteidstriagebyindication.updateValueAndValidity();
      this.reportForm.controls.siteidsstudydetails.setValidators(null)
      this.reportForm.controls.siteidsstudydetails.updateValueAndValidity();
    }

    this.getStudies()
  }
  get getkeys() {
    return Object.keys({
      "regDocsReceived": "2023-02-21",
      "sourceDue": null,
      "sourceComplete": null,
      // "requiredSourceDueAndComplete": false,
      "submittedToSponsor": "2023-02-26",
      "submittedToIrb": null,
      // "requiredSubmittedToIrb": false,
      "irbApproval": null,
      "regBinderReceived": "2023-02-21",
      "delegLogComplete": null,
      "labManualReceived": null,
      "labKitsReceived": null,
      "ekgReceived": null,
      // "requiredEkgReceived": false,
      "laptopReceived": null,
      // "requiredLaptopReceived": false,
      "investigatorMeeting": null,
      // "requiredInvestigatorMeeting": false,
      "initDrugReceived": null,
      "siv": null,
      // "requiredSiv": false,
      "firstMonitorVisit": null,
      "closeoutVisit": null
  });
}
  toggle() {
    this.alldates = !this.alldates;
    this.enrollmentReportPrintView = false;
    this.enrollmentReport = false

    if(this.alldates) {
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.reset('')
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.disable();
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.reset('')
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.disable();
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.setValue('')
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.setValidators(null)
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.updateValueAndValidity();
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.setValue('')
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.setValidators(null)
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.updateValueAndValidity();
    } else {
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.setValue(new Date(JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('scUserSettings'))?.reportsDateFrom == undefined ? '' :JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('scUserSettings'))?.reportsDateFrom))
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.setValidators(null)
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.updateValueAndValidity();
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.setValue(new Date(JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('scUserSettings'))?.reportsDateTo == undefined ? '' :JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('scUserSettings'))?.reportsDateTo))
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.setValidators(null)
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.updateValueAndValidity();
      this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.enable();
      this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.enable();
    }
    this.getStudies()
  }

  toogle2() {
    this.showproviders = !this.showproviders
  } 
  toggle3() {
    this.resetValidators()
    this.reportForm.controls.study.reset('')
    this.showstudyParticipantsReportClosedStudies = !this.showstudyParticipantsReportClosedStudies
    if(this.showstudyParticipantsReportClosedStudies) {
      this.getClosedStudies()
      
    } else {
      this.searcher2('',1,30)
    }
  }

  getStudies() {
    this.studiesloading = true;
    this.enrollmentReportPrintView = false;
    this.enrollmentReport = false
    this.reportForm.controls.study.reset('')
    this.reportForm.controls.study.updateValueAndValidity()
   
    if(this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id != 'null') {

      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'SCREEN_REPORT' ) {
        this.getStudies2(); //statuses endpoint
      } else if (this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'VISIT_PROJECTIONS_REPORT')  {
        this.getActiveStudies()
      } else if (this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'STUDY_PARTICIPANTS_REPORT')  {
        if(this.showstudyParticipantsReportClosedStudies) {
          this.getClosedStudies()
        } else {
          this.searcher2('',1,30)
        }
      }else if (this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'WAITLISTED_PATIENTS_REPORT')  {
        this.getDenovoStudies()
      } else  {
        this.searcher2('',1,30)
      }
      this.refreshusers(this.reportForm.controls.site.value)
    }
  }


  getStudiesForProjections() {
    this.userPreferences.setuserState('selectedSite',this.reportForm.controls.site.value,true)
    this.studyLastActivity = []
    this.studyLastActivityCopy = []
    const data = {
      siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,trialType: '',
      dateFrom: this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ?  '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,
      dateTo: this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') , 
    }
    this.trackedVisitService.getVisitsForProjectionsReport(data).subscribe(res => {
   
        this.studyLastActivityCopy = [...res];
        this.studyLastActivity =[...res]
      this.studiesloading = false;

    }, err => {
      this.studiesloading = false;
    })
  }
  getActiveStudies() {
    this.userPreferences.setuserState('selectedSite',this.reportForm.controls.site.value,true)
    this.studyLastActivity = []
    this.studyLastActivityCopy = []
    const data = {
      search:'',
      pageNumber: 0,
     pageSize: 1000,
      siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
      statuses:['ACTIVE']
    }
    this.siteService.getStudies(data).subscribe(res => {
      this.studyLastActivity = [...this.studyLastActivity,...res?.content]
      this.studyLastActivityCopy =  [...this.studyLastActivityCopy,...res?.content] 
      this.studiesloading = false;

    }, err => {
      this.studiesloading = false;
    })
  }

getDenovoStudies() {
  this.appointmentService.getDenovoStudies({pageSize:200,pageNumber:0,siteId:this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,statuses:['MOVING_FORWARD','ACTIVE'],search:''}).subscribe(res=> {
    this.denovostudies = []
    this.denovostudies =[...this.denovostudies,...res]
    this.denovostudiescopy = []
    this.denovostudiescopy =[...this.denovostudiescopy,...res]
    this.studiesloading = false;
  },err =>{
    this.studiesloading = false;

  })

}

  getStudies2() {
    this.userPreferences.setuserState('selectedSite',this.reportForm.controls.site.value,true)
    this.studyLastActivity = []
    this.studyLastActivityCopy = []
    const data = {
      search:'',
      pageNumber: 0,
     pageSize: 1000,
      siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
      statuses:['MOVING_FORWARD','ADD_ON','ACTIVE']
    }
    this.siteService.getStudies(data).subscribe(res => {
      this.studyLastActivity = []
      this.studyLastActivity =[...this.studyLastActivity,...res.content]
      this.studyLastActivityCopy = []
      this.studyLastActivityCopy =[...this.studyLastActivityCopy,...res.content]
      this.studiesloading = false;

    }, err => {
      this.studiesloading = false;
    })
  }
  getClosedStudies() {
    this.userPreferences.setuserState('selectedSite',this.reportForm.controls.site.value,true)
    this.studyLastActivity = []
    this.studyLastActivityCopy = []
    const data = {
      search:'',
      pageNumber: 0,
     pageSize: 1000,
      siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
      statuses:['SPONSOR_CLOSED','ACTIVE','COMPLETED']
    }
    this.siteService.getStudies(data).subscribe(res => {
      this.studyLastActivity = []
      this.studyLastActivity =[...this.studyLastActivity,...res.content]
      this.studyLastActivityCopy = []
      this.studyLastActivityCopy =[...this.studyLastActivityCopy,...res.content]
      this.studiesloading = false;

    }, err => {
      this.studiesloading = false;
    })
  }

  printPreview(){
    if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'ENROLLMENT_LOGS') {
      this.enrollmentReportPrintView = !this.enrollmentReportPrintView;
    }
    if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'STUDY_PARTICIPANTS_REPORT') {
      this.studyParticipantsReportprint = !this.studyParticipantsReportprint;
    }
  }

  openPatientMiniViewDialog(patient) {
  
  
    if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'STUDY_PARTICIPANTS_REPORT') {
      patient.id = patient?.patient_id
    }
    if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'VISIT_PROJECTIONS_REPORT') {
      patient.patientFullName = patient?.alias
    } 
    if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'SMS_LOGS') {
      patient.id = patient?.patientId
    }   
  
    const ref = this.dialog.open(PatientMiniViewDialogComponent, {
      width: 'auto',
       maxHeight:'80vh',
      panelClass:'custom-dialog-container',
      maxWidth:'80vw',      
      minWidth:'62rem',
      height:'auto',
      disableClose: true,
      data: {
        fromTracking:false,
        patient,
        site:{id:this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id},
      }
    });
  }

  percentage(percent, total) {
    if(total == 0 && percent == 0) return 0
    return ((percent/ total) * 100).toFixed(2);
  }

  toggleTable(type) {
    if(type == 0) {
      this.showCalls = !this.showCalls 
    }
    if(type == 1) {
      this.showWebappt = !this.showWebappt 
    }
    
    if(type == 2) {
      this.showAnscalls = !this.showAnscalls 
    }
    if(type == 3) {
      this.showDBCalls = !this.showDBCalls 
    }
  }
  generate() {
    this.loading = true;

    if(this.reportForm.valid) {
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'STUDY_DETAILS_REPORT') {
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('studyDetailReportStatuses',this.reportForm.controls.statuses.value)

        const data = {siteIds: this.reportForm.controls.siteidsstudydetails.value.includes(0)  ? [...this.sites.map(elem => elem.id)] : [...this.reportForm.controls.siteidsstudydetails.value.map(elem => {
          if(elem != 0) return elem;
        }) ],
          statuses: this.reportForm.controls.statuses.value
        }
        this.triageService.studyDetailReport(data).subscribe(res => {
          this.studyBuildReport = res;
          this.studyBuildReportcopy = res;
          this.studydetailmovfw = []
          this.studydetailmovfwcopy = []
          this.studydetailsaddon = []
          this.studydetailsaddoncopy = []
          this.studydetailscompleted = []
          this.studydetailscompletedcopy = []
          this.studydetailsactive = []
          this.studydetailsactivecopy = []
          this.nogroups ={
            completed:true,
            movingfw:true,
            active:true,
            addon:true,
          }
          this.studyBuildReport.forEach(elem => {
            if(elem.studyStatus =='ACTIVE') {
              this.nogroups.active = false;
              this.studydetailsactive.push(elem)
              this.studydetailsactivecopy.push(elem)
            }
            if(elem.studyStatus =='COMPLETED' || elem.studyStatus =='SPONSOR_CLOSED') {
              this.nogroups.completed = false;
              this.studydetailscompleted.push(elem)
              this.studydetailscompletedcopy.push(elem)


            }
            if(elem.studyStatus =='MOVING_FORWARD') {
              this.nogroups.movingfw = false;
              this.studydetailmovfw.push(elem)
              this.studydetailmovfwcopy.push(elem)

            }
            if(elem.studyStatus =='ADD_ON') {
              this.nogroups.addon = false;
              this.studydetailsaddon.push(elem)
              this.studydetailsaddoncopy.push(elem)

            }
          })
          this.rendered = true;
          this.loading = false;

        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;
        })
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'STUDY_START_UP_REPORT') {
this.studystartupreport = false;
this.studystartupreportdetails = []
        const data = { siteIds: this.reportForm.controls.siteidsstudystartup.value.includes(0)  ? [...this.sites.map(elem => elem.id)] : [...this.reportForm.controls.siteidsstudystartup.value.map(elem => {
          if(elem != 0) return elem;
        }) ]
        }
        this.triageService.getStudyStartUpReport(data.siteIds).subscribe(res => {
          this.studystartupreportdetails = res;
          const groupedData = {};

          this.studystartupreportdetails.forEach(item => {
              const siteAlias = item.siteAlias;
              const studyName = item;

              if (!groupedData[siteAlias]) {
                  groupedData[siteAlias] = [];
              }

              groupedData[siteAlias].push(studyName);
          });

          const result = {};

          let index = 0;
          for (const siteAlias in groupedData) {
              result[`${siteAlias}`] = [...groupedData[siteAlias].map(elem => elem)];
          }

            this.studystartupreportdetails = result;
            this.studystartupreport = true;
          this.loading = false;

        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;
        })
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'WAITLISTED_PATIENTS_REPORT' ) {
        this.waitlistReportDetails = [];
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateFrom',this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value)
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)
        const data = {
          siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
          interestId: this.reportForm.controls.waitlistindications.value != '' ?this.reportForm.controls.waitlistindications.value.id :'',
          interestStudyId: this.reportForm.controls.study?.value?.id ?  this.reportForm.controls.study?.value?.id : '',
          dateFrom: this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ?  '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,
          dateTo: this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') , 
        }
        this.triageService.gerWaitlistPatientReport(data).subscribe(res => {
          this.waitlistReportDetails = res;
          this.dataSource = new MatTableDataSource(res.waitlistByInterest);
          this.dataSource.paginator = this.paginator;
          this.dataSource.sort = this.sort;
          this.dataSource2 = new MatTableDataSource(res.waitlistByStudies);
          this.dataSource2.paginator = this.paginator2;
          this.dataSource2.sort = this.sort2;
          this.waitlistReport = true;
          this.loading = false;

        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;

        })
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'SCHEDULED_SCREEN_REPORT') {
        this.scheduleScreenReport = [];
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateFrom',this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value)
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)
        this.triageService.getScreenScheduledReport( this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id).subscribe(res => {
          this.scheduleScreenReport = res;
          this.scheduleScreen = true;
          this.loading = false;

        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;
        })
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'DAILY_CALLS_REPORT') {
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateFrom',this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value)
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)
        this.dailyCallsReportDetails = [];
        this.dailyCallsReportDetailscalls = [];
        this.dailyCallsReportDetailswebapp = [];
        this.dailyCallsReportDetailsanswcall = [];
        this.dailyCallsReportDetailsdatabase = [];
        this.showCalls = false;
        this.showWebappt = false;
        this.showDBCalls = false;
        this.showAnscalls = false;
        this.allLoaded = false;;
        const data = {
          siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
           dateFrom: this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ?  '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,
          dateTo: this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') , 
        }
        this.triageService.getDailyCallsReportSummary(data).subscribe(res => {
          this.dailyCallsReportDetailsSummary = res;

          const r0 = this.triageService.getDailyCallsReportInfoCalls(data);
          const r1 = this.triageService.getDailyCallsReportWebAppointments(data);
          const r2 =  this.triageService.getDailyCallsReportDatabaseCalls(data);
          const r3 = this.triageService.getDailyCallsReportAnsweringService(data);
          forkJoin([r0,r1,r2,r3]).subscribe(res =>{ 
              this.dailyCallsReport = true;
              this.dailyCallsReportDetailscalls = res[0];
              this.dailyCallsReportDetailswebapp = res[1];
              this.dailyCallsReportDetailsdatabase = res[2];
              this.dailyCallsReportDetailsanswcall = res[3];
              this.dailyCallsReportDetails = [...this.dailyCallsReportDetailscalls,...this.dailyCallsReportDetailswebapp,...this.dailyCallsReportDetailsdatabase,...this.dailyCallsReportDetailsanswcall];
              this.loading = false;
              this.allLoaded = true;

            }, err => {
              this.loading = false;
            })
             
          this.loading = false;
         this.dailyCallsReport = true;
         } )
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'CALL/PS_CONVERSION_REPORT') {
        this.psconversionReportDetails = [];
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateFrom',this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value)
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)
        const data = {
          siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value?.id,
          interestIds: this.reportForm.controls.indications.value != '' ?[this.reportForm.controls.indications.value.map(elem => elem.id)] :'',
          dateFrom: this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ?  '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,
          dateTo: this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') , 
        }
        this.triageService.getCallsPSReport(data).subscribe(res => {
          this.psconversionReportDetails = res;
          this.psconvtotals = {
            callPsRatio:0,
            psCompleted:0,
            psScheduled:0,
            psScheduledCompletedRatio:0,
            calls:0
          }
          this.psconversionReportDetails.forEach(element => {
            this.psconvtotals.psCompleted += parseFloat(element.psCompleted)
            this.psconvtotals.psScheduled += parseFloat(element.psScheduled)
            this.psconvtotals.calls += parseFloat(element.calls)
          });
          this.psconvtotals.callPsRatio = Math.fround( (this.psconvtotals.psCompleted / this.psconvtotals.calls) *100)
          this.psconvtotals.psScheduledCompletedRatio = Math.fround( (this.psconvtotals.psCompleted / this.psconvtotals.psScheduled) *100)
          this.psconversionReport = true;

          this.loading = false;
        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;
        })
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'PRESCREEN_REPORT') {
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateFrom',this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value)
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)
        const data = {
          siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
          dateFrom: this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ?  '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,
          dateTo: this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') , 
          ord1:this.reportForm.controls.ord1.value,
          dir1:this.reportForm.controls.dir1.value,
          ord2:this.reportForm.controls.ord2.value,
          dir2:this.reportForm.controls.dir2.value,
          ord3:this.reportForm.controls.ord3.value,
          dir3:this.reportForm.controls.dir3.value,
        }
        this.triageService.prescreenReport(data).subscribe(res => {
          this.psReportDetails = Object.assign([], res)
          this.pstable =new TableData<any>(this.displayedColumns);
          this.pstable.dataSource = new MatMultiSortTableDataSource(this.sort4,true)
          res.forEach(element => {
            element.range = this.getBusinessDatesCount(element.callDate,element.appointmentDate)
          });
          this.pstable.dataSource.data =res;
          this.pstable.dataSource.sort = this.sort4;
          this.pstable.totalElements = res?.length;
          this.pstable.dataSource.orderData = (event?) => {this.sortData(event,0)}
          this.psReport = true;

          this.loading = false;
          this.ref.detectChanges();

        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;
        })
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'SCREEN_REPORT') {
          this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateFrom',this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value)
          this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)
        const data = {
          siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
          studyId: this.reportForm.controls.study.value.id == undefined ? null :  this.reportForm.controls.study.value.id,
          dateFrom: formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value ==null ? new Date(): this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value , 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us'),
          dateTo: formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value == null ? new Date(new Date().setFullYear(new Date().getFullYear() + 5)) : this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value , 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us'),
          ord1:this.reportForm.controls.ord1.value,
          dir1:this.reportForm.controls.dir1.value,
          ord2:this.reportForm.controls.ord2.value,
          dir2:this.reportForm.controls.dir2.value,
          ord3:this.reportForm.controls.ord3.value,
          dir3:this.reportForm.controls.dir3.value,
        
        }
        this.triageService.screenReport(data).subscribe(res => {
          this.scrReportDetails  =Object.assign([], res);
          this.scrtable = new TableData<any>(this.displayedColumns2);
          this.scrtable.dataSource = new MatMultiSortTableDataSource(this.sort3,true)
          this.scrtable.dataSource.data =res;
          this.scrtable.totalElements = res?.length;
          this.scrtable.dataSource.sort = this.sort3;
          this.scrtable.dataSource.orderData = (event?) => {this.sortData(event,1)}
          this.scrReport = true;
          this.loading = false;
          this.ref.detectChanges();

        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;
        })
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'UNTRACKED_VISITS_REPORT') {
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateFrom',this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value)
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)
        this.untrackedVisitsReport = [];
        const data = {
          siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
          dateFrom: this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ?  '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,
          dateTo: this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') , 
        }
        this.triageService.untrackedVisitsReport(data).subscribe(res => {
          this.untrackedVisitsReport =res;
          this.untrackedVisits = true;

          this.loading = false;
        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;
        })
      }
      if(this.reportForm.controls.type.value == 'UNTRACKED_SCREENS_REPORT') {
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateFrom',this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value)
        this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)
        this.untrackedScreensReport= [];
        const data = {
          siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
          dateFrom: this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ?  '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,

            }

          this.totals.prescreentoscreenratio = isNaN(Math.fround( (this.totals.actualscreen / this.totals.actualprescreen) *100)) ? 0 : Math.fround( (this.totals.actualscreen / this.totals.actualprescreen) *100)

   this.cnstypetotals.callpsratio = isNaN(Math.fround( (this.cnstypetotals.actualprescreen / this.cnstypetotals.calls) *100)) ? 0 :Math.fround( (this.cnstypetotals.actualprescreen / this.cnstypetotals.calls) *100)
          this.cnstypetotals.prescreentoscreenratio = isNaN(Math.fround( (this.cnstypetotals.actualscreen / this.cnstypetotals.actualprescreen) *100)) ? 0 : Math.fround( (this.cnstypetotals.actualscreen / this.cnstypetotals.actualprescreen) *100)

          this.medicaltypetotals.prescreentoscreenratio = isNaN(Math.fround( (this.medicaltypetotals.actualscreen / this.medicaltypetotals.actualprescreen) *100)) ? 0 : Math.fround( (this.medicaltypetotals.actualscreen / this.medicaltypetotals.actualprescreen) *100)

          this.vaccinetypetotals.prescreentoscreenratio = isNaN(Math.fround( (this.vaccinetypetotals.actualscreen / this.vaccinetypetotals.actualprescreen) *100)) ? 0 : Math.fround( (this.vaccinetypetotals.actualscreen / this.vaccinetypetotals.actualprescreen) *100)


          this.loading = false;

          dateTo: this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value == '' ? '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,

        this.advertisingService.studyActivityReport(data).subscribe(res => {
         let temp = res;
       
         this.sitenr = temp[0]?.studyDetailReportDto?.siteNr
         this.sitealias = temp[0]?.studyDetailReportDto?.siteValue
         this.trackedVisitService.getVisitsByStudyId(temp[0].studyDetailReportDto.id).subscribe(res1 => {
          this.visits = res1;
          this.visitmatrix.push([])
          this.visits.map((elem, visitindex) => {
            this.counts.push(0);
            this.sums.push(0);
          })
          const data = {
            studyId: temp[0].studyDetailReportDto.id,
            procedureTypeFilter:'ALL_PROCEDURES' ,
            dateFrom: this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value == '' ?  '' : formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us') ,

            patientStudyLinkIds: ''
          }
          this.trackedVisitService.getTrackedVisits(data).subscribe(res2 => {
            this.patientsCopy = res2;
              this.patientsCopy.map(() => {
                this.visitmatrix.push([])
              this.hsums.push(0);
            });
              this.visits.map((visit,j) => {
              
            this.patientsCopy.map((patient:{trackedVisits:any[]},i) => {
                this.visitmatrix[i][j] = []
                let visitadded = false
                patient.trackedVisits?.map(patientVisit => {
                if(patientVisit.masterStudyVisitId == visit.masterStudyVisitId) {
                    visitadded = true;
                    this.visitmatrix[i][j].push(patientVisit);
                  }
                })
                if(!visitadded) this.visitmatrix[i][j] = null;
              })
            })
                  this.sums.fill(0);
                  this.counts.fill(0);
                  this.hsums.fill(0)
                  this.getTotals()
            }, err => {
              this.loading = false;
            })
        });
       
        }, err => {
          this.loading = false;
        })

          this.userPreferences.setuserState('reportsDateTo',this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value,true)

            this.counts2.push(0);
            this.sums2.push(0);
          })
          this.visitmatrix2.push([]);

          this.patientsCopy2.map(() => {
          
            this.hsums2.push(0);
              this.visitmatrix2.push([])});
          this.patientsCopy2.map((patient:{detailedVisits:any[]},i) => {
            this.visits2.map((visit,j) => {
              this.visitmatrix2[i][j] = []
              let visitadded = false
              patient.detailedVisits?.map(patientVisit => {
                  if(patientVisit.masterStudyVisitId == visit.masterStudyVisitId) {
                  visitadded = true;

                  this.visitmatrix2[i][j].push(patientVisit);
                }
              })
              if(!visitadded) this.visitmatrix2[i][j] = null;
            })
          })

                this.sums2.fill(0);
                this.counts2.fill(0);
                this.hsums2.fill(0)

          this.loading = false;

          this.loading = false;

getSiteAliases(ids) {

let temp = []

  if(ids.includes(0)) {

   return 'Consolidated '}

  else { ids.map(id => {this.sites.map(elem => {if(elem?.id == id) temp.push(elem?.alias)})})
  return temp.join(',')+' '
  }
  

}

  onScroll(){
    this.scrollloading = true;
    const data = {
      siteId: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
      errorCodes:this.reportForm.controls.errorCodes.value.includes(0) ? this.reportForm.controls.errorCodes.value.filter(elem => elem != 0): this.reportForm.controls.errorCodes.value  ,
      smsOutboundTypes: this.reportForm.controls.smstype.value.includes(0) ? this.reportForm.controls.smstype.value.filter(elem => elem != 0): this.reportForm.controls.smstype.value  ,
      plivoStatuses: this.reportForm.controls.plivostatus.value.includes(0) ? this.reportForm.controls.plivostatus.value.filter(elem => elem != 0): this.reportForm.controls.plivostatus.value ,
      skip: (this.smsactualpage * 30) ,
      limit: 30 ,
      dateFrom: formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateFrom.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us'),
      dateTo: formatDate(this.reportForm.controls.dateTo.value, 'yyyy-MM-dd', 'en-Us'),
    }
    this.triageService.getSMSLogReport(data).subscribe(res=> {
      res?.forEach(elem =>{
this.failedsmsdetails.push(elem)
      })
      this.smsactualpage++;
      this.scrollloading = false
      this.failedsmsdetailsreport=true;
    })
    this.cdr.detectChanges();
  }
  getTotals2(){
    if(this.visitprojectioncountedvisit) {
      this.visitmatrix2.forEach((elem,i) =>{
        elem.forEach((visit ,i3)=> {
          if(visit != null ) {
            visit.forEach((p,i2) => {
              if(this.visits2[i3]?.countVisit == true){
                this.hsums2[i]++

              }
            })
          }
        })
      })
      for(let i = 0; i<this.visits2.length; i++) {
        this.counts2[i]= this.getColumnCount2(i);
      }
      this.ttotal2.visits = this.hsums2.reduce((partialSum, a) => partialSum + a, 0);
      this.loading = false;
      this.visitprojectionsReport = true;
    } else {
      this.visitmatrix2.forEach((elem,i) =>{
        elem.forEach(visit => {
          if(visit != null) {
            visit.forEach(p => {
              this.hsums2[i]++
            })
          }
        })
      })
      for(let i = 0; i<this.visits2.length; i++) {
        this.counts2[i]= this.getColumnCount2(i);
      }
      this.ttotal2.visits = this.counts2.reduce((partialSum, a) => partialSum + a, 0);
      this.loading = false;
      this.visitprojectionsReport = true;
    }
    
  }
  sortDatastudyDetailsaddon(sort){
    const data = this.studydetailsaddon;
    if (!sort.active || sort.direction === '') {
      this.sortedData = data;
      return;
    }
    this.sortedData = data.sort((a, b) => {
      const isAsc = sort.direction === 'asc';
      switch (sort.active) {
        case 'protocol':
          return this.compare(a.protocolName?.toLowerCase(), b.protocolName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'indication':
          return this.compare(a.indicationName?.toLowerCase(), b.indicationName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
          case 'PI':
            return this.compare(a.principalInvestigatorFullName?.toLowerCase(), b.principalInvestigatorFullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
          case 'leadcrc':
            return this.compare(a.leadCrcFullName?.toLowerCase(), b.leadCrcFullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'backupcrc':
            return this.compare(a.backupCrcFullName?.toLowerCase(), b.backupCrcFullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'backupcrc2':
            return this.compare(a.backupCrc2FullName?.toLowerCase(), b.backupCrc2FullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'sitenumber':
            return this.compare(a.siteNr, b.siteNr, isAsc);
       case 'irb':
            return this.compare(a.irbName?.toLowerCase(), b.irbName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'lab':
            return this.compare(a.labName?.toLowerCase(), b.labName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'status':
            return this.compare(a.studyStatus?.toLowerCase(), b.studyStatus?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'site':
            return this.compare(a.siteValueAlias?.toLowerCase(), b.siteValueAlias?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'sponsor':
            return this.compare(a.sponsorName?.toLowerCase(), b.sponsorName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       
      }
    });
  }
  sortDatastudyDetailscomp(sort){
    const data = this.studydetailscompleted;
    if (!sort.active || sort.direction === '') {
      this.sortedData = data;
      return;
    }
    this.sortedData = data.sort((a, b) => {
      const isAsc = sort.direction === 'asc';
      switch (sort.active) {
        case 'protocol':
          return this.compare(a.protocolName?.toLowerCase(), b.protocolName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'indication':
          return this.compare(a.indicationName?.toLowerCase(), b.indicationName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
          case 'PI':
            return this.compare(a.principalInvestigatorFullName?.toLowerCase(), b.principalInvestigatorFullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
          case 'leadcrc':
            return this.compare(a.leadCrcFullName?.toLowerCase(), b.leadCrcFullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'backupcrc':
            return this.compare(a.backupCrcFullName?.toLowerCase(), b.backupCrcFullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'backupcrc2':
            return this.compare(a.backupCrc2FullName?.toLowerCase(), b.backupCrc2FullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       case 'sitenumber':

  getColumnCount2(j) {
    let count = 0
    for(let i = 0; i<this.visitmatrix2.length; i++) {
      if(this.visitmatrix2[i][j]!=null) {
        this.visitmatrix2[i][j].forEach(element => {
          count++
        });
      }
    }
    return count;

  }
  getTotals(){
    this.visitmatrix.forEach((elem,i) =>{
      elem.forEach(visit => {
        if(visit != null) {
          visit.forEach(p => {
            this.hsums[i]++
          })
        }
      })
    })
    for(let i = 0; i<this.visits.length; i++) {
      this.counts[i]= this.getColumnCount(i);
    }
    this.ttotal.visits = this.counts.reduce((partialSum, a) => partialSum + a, 0);
    this.loading = false;
    this.enrollmentReport = true;
  }

 

  getColumnCount(j) {
    let count = 0
    for(let i = 0; i<this.visitmatrix.length; i++) {
      if(this.visitmatrix[i][j]!=null) {
        this.visitmatrix[i][j].forEach(element => {
          count++
        });
      }
    }
    return count;

  }
  filter2(type) {
    if(type==1) {
      this.visitprojectioncountedvisit = true;
      this.visitprojectionallvisits = false;
      this.sums2.fill(0);
      this.counts2.fill(0);
      this.hsums2.fill(0)
      this.getTotals2()
    }
    if(type==0) {
      this.visitprojectioncountedvisit =false;
      this.visitprojectionallvisits = true;
      this.sums2.fill(0);
      this.counts2.fill(0);
      this.hsums2.fill(0)
      this.getTotals2()
    }
  }
  add(y, z) {
    return  +y + +z;
  }
  
  sortData(event,type) {
    let result;

    if(type) {
      const temp = Object.assign([], this.scrReportDetails);
      if (this.scrtable.sortParams.length === 0) {
        result = temp
      } else if (this.scrtable.sortParams.length > 0) {
        
        const sorted = temp.sort((u1, u2) => {
          return this._sortData(u1, u2, this.scrtable.sortParams, this.scrtable.sortDirs);
        });
        result = sorted
        this.scrtable.dataSource.data = result;
        this.ref.detectChanges();

      }
    } else {
      const temp = Object.assign([], this.psReportDetails);
      if (this.pstable.sortParams.length === 0) {
        result = temp
      } else if (this.pstable.sortParams.length > 0) {
        
        const sorted = temp.sort((u1, u2) => {
          return this._sortData(u1, u2, this.pstable.sortParams, this.pstable.sortDirs);
        });
        result = sorted
        this.pstable.dataSource.data = result;
        this.ref.detectChanges();

      }
    }

  }
  getBusinessDatesCount(startDate, endDate) {
    startDate = new Date(startDate);
    endDate = new Date(endDate);

    let count = 0;
    const curDate = new Date(startDate.getTime());
    while (curDate <= endDate) {
        const dayOfWeek = curDate.getDay();
        if(dayOfWeek !== 0 && dayOfWeek !== 6) count++;
        curDate.setDate(curDate.getDate() + 1);
    }
    
    return count;
}
sortDataSimple(sort: Sort) {
  const data = this.dailyCallsReportDetails;
  if (!sort.active || sort.direction === '') {
    this.sortedData = data;
    return;
  }
  this.sortedData = data.sort((a, b) => {
    const isAsc = sort.direction === 'asc';
    switch (sort.active) {
      case 'call-date-time':
        return this.compare(new Date(a.callDateTime).getTime(), new Date(b.callDateTime).getTime(), isAsc);
      case 'outcome':
        return this.compare(a.outcomeCategory?.toLowerCase(), b.outcomeCategory?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'ad-source':
          return this.compare(a.adSource?.toLowerCase(), b.adSource?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'indication':
          return this.compare(a.indicationName?.toLowerCase(), b.indicationName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
       
    }
  });
}
sortDataUntrackedVisits(sort: Sort) {
  const data = this.untrackedVisitsReport;
  if (!sort.active || sort.direction === '') {
    this.sortedData = data;
    return;
  }
  this.sortedData = data.sort((a, b) => {
    const isAsc = sort.direction === 'asc';
    switch (sort.active) {
      case 'alias':
        return this.compare(a.alias?.toLowerCase(), b.alias?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
      case 'providers':
        return this.compare(a.providerUsers[0].firstName?.toLowerCase()+a.providerUsers[0].lastName?.toLowerCase() || a.providerResources[0].name?.toLowerCase(),b.providerUsers[0].firstName?.toLowerCase()+b.providerUsers[0].lastName?.toLowerCase() || b.providerResources[0].name?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'apptdate':
          return this.compare(new Date(a.appointmentDate).getTime(), new Date(b.appointmentDate).getTime(), isAsc);
        case 'study':
          return this.compare(a.studyName?.toLowerCase(), b.studyName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'visitname':
          return this.compare(a.studyVisitName?.toLowerCase(), b.studyVisitName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'noshow':
        return this.compare(a.noShow, b.noShow, isAsc);
    }
  });
}

sortDataReschedules(sort: Sort) {
  const data = this.rescheduledAppointmentsReport;
  if (!sort.active || sort.direction === '') {
    this.sortedData = data;
    return;
  }
  this.sortedData = data.sort((a, b) => {
    const isAsc = sort.direction === 'asc';
    switch (sort.active) {
      case 'actiondate':
          return this.compare(new Date(a.actionDate).getTime(), new Date(b.actionDate).getTime(), isAsc);
       case 'createdby':
          return this.compare(a.createdByFullName?.toLowerCase(), b.createdByFullName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'datefrom':
          return this.compare(new Date(a.fromDate).getTime(), new Date(b.fromDate).getTime(), isAsc);
        case 'dateto':
          return this.compare(new Date(a.toDate).getTime(), new Date(b.toDate).getTime(), isAsc);
        case 'reschedulenr':
           return this.compare(a.numberOfReschedules, b.numberOfReschedules, isAsc);
        case 'reason':
            return this.compare(a.reasonName?.toLowerCase(), b.reasonName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);    
        case 'study':
            return this.compare(a?.studyName, b?.studyName, isAsc);
        case 'appttype':
            return this.compare(a.appointmentType?.toLowerCase(), b.appointmentType?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'patientname':
            return this.compare(a.patientName?.toLowerCase(), b.patientName?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
        case 'interest':
          return this.compare(a.patientInterestNames[0]?.toLowerCase(), b.patientInterestNames[0]?.toLowerCase(), isAsc);
                    
    }
  });
}

       case 'calls':

        case 'psCompleted':

    }
  });
}
compare(a: number | string, b: number | string, isAsc: boolean) {
  return (a < b ? -1 : 1) * (isAsc ? 1 : -1);
}

    });
  }
 
  toggleFullTable() {
    this.enrollfulltable = !this.enrollfulltable
    this.userPreferences.setuserState('enrollmentReportFullTable',this.enrollfulltable)
  }

  populateselectedindication(selectdom){
    if(selectdom.selected?.length) {
      this.indications= this.selectedIndications;
      this.indications.forEach(elem => {
        elem.value = elem.id
      })
    } else {
      this.selectedIndications = []
    }
  }
  saveSelectedindication(event){
    const value = event.value as any[];
    if (event.source.selected.length) {
      if(this.selectedIndications.indexOf(value) == -1) {
        this.selectedIndications = [...value]
        this.reportForm.controls.indications.setValue(this.selectedIndications);
        this.reportForm.controls.indications.setValue(this.selectedIndications);
      }
    } else {
      const index = this.selectedIndications.indexOf(value);
      if (index !== -1) {
        this.selectedIndications.splice(index, 1);
      }
    }
  }

  get getkeys2() {
    return Object.keys(this.studystartupreportdetails)
  }
  openCreateWorkingListDialog(){
    if(!this.allCheck){
      const selected = []
      this.patientChecks.map((elem,i) => {
        if(elem) {
            selected.push(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[i].patient_id);
        }
      });
      const ref =  this.dialog.open(CreateWorkingListFromCheckboxesDialogComponent, {
        data: {
          addPatient: false,
          site: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
          allPatients:false,
          selectedPatients:selected,
        },
        width: 'auto',
        height: 'auto',
        disableClose: true,
        maxHeight:'80vh',
        maxWidth:'70vw',
        panelClass:'custom-dialog-container',
      });
    } else {  const selected = []
      this.patientChecks.map((elem,i) => {
            selected.push(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[i].patient_id);
      });
      const ref =  this.dialog.open(CreateWorkingListFromCheckboxesDialogComponent, {
        data: {
          addPatient: false,
          site: this.reportForm.controls.site.value.id,
          allPatients:false,
          selectedPatients:selected,
        },
        width: 'auto',
        height: 'auto',
        disableClose: true,
        maxHeight:'80vh',
        maxWidth:'70vw',
        panelClass:'custom-dialog-container',
      });
    }
   
  }

  toogleAll(status) {
    this.allCheck = status;
    this.excludedPatients = [];
    this.selectedPatients = []
    for(let i =0; i< this.patientChecks.length; i++) {
    
      if(!this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[i]?.doNotContact) {

        this.patientChecks[i] =status;
      } else {
        this.excludedPatients.push(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[i].patient_id)
        this.patientChecks[i] =false
      }
    }
  }
  
 

  toggleStatus(status, index) {
    if(this.allCheck) {
      this.patientChecks[index] = status;
      if(!status) {
        if(this.excludedPatients.indexOf(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[index].patient_id) == -1 ) {
          this.excludedPatients.push(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[index].patient_id);
        }
      } else {
        this.excludedPatients.splice(this.excludedPatients.indexOf(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[index].patient_id),1)
      }
    } else {
      this.patientChecks[index] = status;
      if(status) {
        if(this.selectedPatients.indexOf(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[index].patient_id) == -1 ) {
          this.selectedPatients.push(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[index].patient_id);
        }
      } else {
       this.selectedPatients.splice(this.selectedPatients.indexOf(this.studyParticipantsReportDetails[index].patient_id),1)
      }
    }


  }

                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">30</td>
                                              <td>Spam Detected</td>
                                              <td>
                                                 <p>One of the most common reasons for SMS delivery failure is carrier-level spam filters. Carriers have added systems and algorithms to detect spam content and block messages before they get delivered. Unfortunately, these filters are always hidden, are subject to carrier preferences, vary from carrier to carrier, and can be changed without notice.</p>
                                                 <p>Another common reason why this error code could be returned is that you may have attempted to send too many messages using long code phone numbers in the US and Canada. Long codes are 10-digit phone numbers and are intended for person-to-person (P2P) communication.</p>
                                                 <p>If you get this error frequently, we recommend you use short codes for sending bulk messages within the US and Canada.</p>

                                              <td>Invalid Source Number</td>

Check the src phone number in your application and ensure that it's in the correct format and has the ability to send text messages.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">50</td>
                                              <td>Invalid Destination Number</td>
                                              <td>The destination number you entered is either not entered correctly, not SMS-enabled, or is a PSTN landline. Check the dst phone number in your application to ensure that it's able to receive text messages. If you're sending multiple text messages, make sure that the phone numbers are separated with the &lt; character (e.g., 14156667777&lt;14157778888&lt;14158889999).</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">60</td>
                                              <td>Loop Detected</td>
                                              <td>The carrier is not able to route your SMS because certain settings in your application create an endless loop of messages being sent and received between your src and dst phone numbers. This can occur when two autoresponding SMS applications start to talk to each other. Carriers detect loops by comparing messages sent and received within a predefined period of time to previous messages, though not all carriers have loop detection. SMS loops increase unnecessary spend, so to ensure that your applications don't trigger loops, it's a good idea to create loop filters in your applications. In some cases, this error code is returned when the carrier determines that it's impossible to route the message, so it has to be dropped as it's being looped between platforms.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">70</td>
                                              <td>Destination Permanently Unavailable</td>
                                              <td>The destination (dst) phone number is not active and there is no indication of when it will become available again. This is a broad error code that's generated when the carrier hasn't indicated the reason for the destination unavailability. Check the dst phone number to ensure that it's correct. Also, try sending messages to an alternative number to ensure that all other parts of your application are working.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">80</td>
                                              <td>Destination Temporarily Unavailable</td>
                                              <td>The destination (dst) phone number is not reachable. This is a broad error code, and often the carrier doesn't indicate the reason for the destination to be temporarily unavailable. Possible reasons may include a handset being turned off or out of coverage. To resolve this problem, retry your messages later.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">90</td>
                                              <td>No Route Available</td>
                                              <td>The carrier and fallback carriers were not able to deliver the SMS message because no route was available. Carriers don't provide a reason why a route is unavailable, but this is typically a carrier issue. </td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">100</td>
                                              <td>Prohibited by Carrier</td>
                                              <td>The carrier rejected the message because the network didn't support the message being sent. This can occur if the destination network doesn't support SMS.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">110</td>
                                              <td>Message Too Long</td>
                                              <td>The message content exceeds the limit of 1,600 characters for GSM-encoded messages and 737 for UCS-2-encoded messages. Note that depending on the byte size, emoji characters can also increase the message character count. Plivo automatically concatenates messages longer than 160 characters for GSM-encoded messages and 70 characters for UCS-2-encoded messages.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">150</td>

                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">160</td>
                                              <td>DLT Registration Issue</td>
                                              <td>This message was rejected because of an issue in DLT registration. Ensure you're using only DLT-registered headers and templates. Contact Plivo support if you continue facing this issue.

                                           </tr>

                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">200</td>
                                              <td>Source Number Blocked by STOP from Destination Number</td>
                                              <td>The destination has opted out from your campaign and blocked all messages sent from your phone number. All messages to destinations that have opted out are blocked until the destination opts in with another response. </td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">300</td>
                                              <td>Failed to Dispatch Message</td>
                                              <td>An error was encountered while passing the message to downstream carriers. This is an internal failure; messages with this error code can be retried at a later time. Customers are not charged for messages that fail with this error code.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">420</td>
                                              <td>Message Expired</td>
                                             <td>Messages that remain in Plivo processing queues for longer than three hours are not forwarded to a downstream carrier. </td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">450</td>
                                              <td>Destination Country Disabled</td>
                                              <td>Messages to this destination country have been disabled for your account. To enable them, update your Geo Permission preferences on the console.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">900</td>
                                              <td>Insufficient Credit</td>
                                              <td>Your account does not have the required credits to send this message. Recharge your account and try again.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">910</td>
                                              <td>Account Disabled</td>
                                              <td>The message was rejected because the parent Plivo account was found to be in a disabled state when the message was dequeued for processing.</td>
                                           </tr>
                                           <tr>
                                              <td class="font-weight-bold">950</td>
                                              <td>Daily Messaging Limit Reached for Your 10DLC Brand</td>
                                              <td>T-Mobile (including Sprint and Metro by T-Mobile) has a limit on the total daily messages (TPD) a brand can send toward its subscribers. T-Mobile's TPD limit takes into account both SMS and MMS messages; in other words, the daily limit is shared across SMS and MMS services. This error means you have reached the allotted limit for your brand and all the subsequent messages to T-Mobile (including Sprint and Metro by T-Mobile) will continue to fail for the day. The counter resets each day at midnight Pacific Time, after which you can restart messaging. </td>
                                           </tr>

Unverified numbers have daily, weekly, and monthly limits on the number of messages they can send. This error means you have exceeded those limits and must consider verifying your toll-free number. If your number is already submitted for verification and you see this error, your messages were caught by carrier messaging filters. To initiate a verification request for a single Plivo toll-free number. </td>
